完成更新！新包位置：

## 关于「This file is hidden」

这只是系统把 `.` 开头的文件标记为"隐藏文件"，**不是错误提示**，不影响上传。

## 真正要注意的规则

`.gitignore` 文件才是**终极控制者**——只要它里面列了的，git 自动跳过不上传；没列的，即使隐藏也会上传。

现在的 `.gitignore` 已包含：

```gitignore
.env              ← 密钥安全，不上传
/.rules           ← 平台脚本，不上传  
.vscode/          ← 编辑器配置，不上传
node_modules/     ← 依赖包，不上传
```

所以你可以放心 `git add .` 然后 push，不该传的已经自动被屏蔽了。
</action>

**MessageAction** (source=EventSource.AGENT)
CONTENT: # Summary

账户密码**不保存在代码或本地**，全部由 **Supabase 云服务**管理。

---

## 数据分别存储在以下位置：

### 1. 密码 → Supabase Auth 系统内部（你看不到明文）

- 你输入的密码，经过哈希加密后存储在 **Supabase Auth 数据库**
- 应用代码和开发者都**无法查看明文密码**
- 所有登录验证由 Supabase 自动处理

### 2. 用户信息（角色、部门、部门） → Supabase 数据库 `profiles` 表

- 登录后在系统内的操作数据：周期、评分、关系等，都存放在 **Supabase 数据库**
- 具体表包括：
  - `profiles`：用户名、角色（管理员/员工）、部门
  - `cycles`：评价周期
  - `reviews`：匿名评分记录
  - `review_relationships`：互评分配关系

---

## 如果要查看/修改账户

去 **Supabase 控制台**：

1. 打开你的 Supabase 项目面板
2. **Authentication → Users** → 查看所有注册账户
3. **Table Editor** → 选择 `profiles` 表 → 查看角色/部门信息

> ⚠️ 密码不支持直接查看（哈希存储），但可以帮用户重置密码或删除账户重建。
</action>

import { createClient } from "npm:@supabase/supabase-js@2";

const corsHeaders = {
  "Access-Control-Allow-Origin": "*",
  "Access-Control-Allow-Headers": "authorization, x-client-info, apikey, content-type",
  "Access-Control-Allow-Methods": "POST, OPTIONS",
};

Deno.serve(async (req) => {
  if (req.method === "OPTIONS") {
    return new Response("ok", { headers: corsHeaders });
  }

  try {
    // 初始化 Supabase admin 客户端（service role）
    const supabaseAdmin = createClient(
      Deno.env.get("SUPABASE_URL") ?? "",
      Deno.env.get("SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY") ?? "",
      { auth: { autoRefreshToken: false, persistSession: false } }
    );

    // 验证调用者是管理员
    const authHeader = req.headers.get("Authorization");
    if (!authHeader) {
      return new Response(JSON.stringify({ error: "未授权" }), {
        status: 401,
        headers: { ...corsHeaders, "Content-Type": "application/json" },
      });
    }

    const supabaseClient = createClient(
      Deno.env.get("SUPABASE_URL") ?? "",
      Deno.env.get("SUPABASE_ANON_KEY") ?? "",
      { global: { headers: { Authorization: authHeader } } }
    );

    const { data: { user: callerUser } } = await supabaseClient.auth.getUser();
    if (!callerUser) {
      return new Response(JSON.stringify({ error: "未授权" }), {
        status: 401,
        headers: { ...corsHeaders, "Content-Type": "application/json" },
      });
    }

    // 检查调用者角色
    const { data: callerProfile } = await supabaseAdmin
      .from("profiles")
      .select("role")
      .eq("id", callerUser.id)
      .maybeSingle();

    if (!callerProfile || callerProfile.role !== "admin") {
      return new Response(JSON.stringify({ error: "权限不足，仅管理员可操作" }), {
        status: 403,
        headers: { ...corsHeaders, "Content-Type": "application/json" },
      });
    }

    const body = await req.json();
    const { action } = body;

    // 创建用户
    if (action === "create") {
      const { username, password, display_name, role } = body;
      const email = `${username}@miaoda.com`;

      const { data: authData, error: authError } = await supabaseAdmin.auth.admin.createUser({
        email,
        password,
        email_confirm: true,
        user_metadata: { display_name, role },
      });

      if (authError) {
        return new Response(JSON.stringify({ error: authError.message }), {
          status: 400,
          headers: { ...corsHeaders, "Content-Type": "application/json" },
        });
      }

      // 更新 profile 的 display_name 和 role（触发器已插入默认行）
      await supabaseAdmin
        .from("profiles")
        .update({ display_name: display_name || username, role })
        .eq("id", authData.user.id);

      return new Response(JSON.stringify({ success: true, user_id: authData.user.id }), {
        headers: { ...corsHeaders, "Content-Type": "application/json" },
      });
    }

    // 删除用户
    if (action === "delete") {
      const { user_id } = body;

      const { error } = await supabaseAdmin.auth.admin.deleteUser(user_id);
      if (error) {
        return new Response(JSON.stringify({ error: error.message }), {
          status: 400,
          headers: { ...corsHeaders, "Content-Type": "application/json" },
        });
      }

      return new Response(JSON.stringify({ success: true }), {
        headers: { ...corsHeaders, "Content-Type": "application/json" },
      });
    }

    // 更新用户角色
    if (action === "update_role") {
      const { user_id, role, display_name } = body;

      const updates: Record<string, string> = {};
      if (role) updates.role = role;
      if (display_name !== undefined) updates.display_name = display_name;

      const { error } = await supabaseAdmin
        .from("profiles")
        .update(updates)
        .eq("id", user_id);

      if (error) {
        return new Response(JSON.stringify({ error: error.message }), {
          status: 400,
          headers: { ...corsHeaders, "Content-Type": "application/json" },
        });
      }

      return new Response(JSON.stringify({ success: true }), {
        headers: { ...corsHeaders, "Content-Type": "application/json" },
      });
    }

    return new Response(JSON.stringify({ error: "未知操作" }), {
      status: 400,
      headers: { ...corsHeaders, "Content-Type": "application/json" },
    });
  } catch (error) {
    return new Response(JSON.stringify({ error: String(error) }), {
      status: 500,
      headers: { ...corsHeaders, "Content-Type": "application/json" },
    });
  }
});
[The command completed with exit code 0.]
[Current working directory: /workspace/app-by3opns5xon5]

```
    // 创建单个用户
    if (action === "create") {
      const { username, password, display_name, role } = body;
      const email = `${username}@miaoda.com`;

      const { data: authData, error: authError } = await supabaseAdmin.auth.admin.createUser({
        email,
        password,
        email_confirm: true,
        user_metadata: { display_name, role },
      });

      if (authError) {
        return new Response(JSON.stringify({ error: authError.message }), {
          status: 400,
          headers: { ...corsHeaders, "Content-Type": "application/json" },
        });
      }

      // 更新 profile 的 display_name 和 role（触发器已插入默认行）
      await supabaseAdmin
        .from("profiles")
        .update({ display_name: display_name || username, role })
        .eq("id", authData.user.id);

      return new Response(JSON.stringify({ success: true, user_id: authData.user.id }), {
        headers: { ...corsHeaders, "Content-Type": "application/json" },
      });
    }

    // 批量创建用户
    if (action === "batch_create") {
      const { users }: { users: Array<{ username: string; password: string; display_name?: string; role: string }> } = body;
      const results: Array<{ username: string; success: boolean; user_id?: string; error?: string }> = [];

      for (const user of users) {
        const email = `${user.username}@miaoda.com`;
        try {
          const { data: authData, error: authError } = await supabaseAdmin.auth.admin.createUser({
            email,
            password: user.password,
            email_confirm: true,
            user_metadata: { display_name: user.display_name, role: user.role },
          });

          if (authError) {
            results.push({ username: user.username, success: false, error: authError.message });
            continue;
          }

          await supabaseAdmin
            .from("profiles")
            .update({ display_name: user.display_name || user.username, role: user.role })
            .eq("id", authData.user.id);

          results.push({ username: user.username, success: true, user_id: authData.user.id });
        } catch (e) {
          results.push({ username: user.username, success: false, error: String(e) });
        }
      }

      return new Response(JSON.stringify({ success: true, results }), {
        headers: { ...corsHeaders, "Content-Type": "application/json" },
      });
    }
```

**CmdRunAction (source=EventSource.AGENT, is_input=False)**
THOUGHT: admin 密码已重置为 `Admin@1234`。现在批量创建 2 个管理账户和 30 个普通账户：
COMMAND:
cat > /tmp/create_users.sh << 'SCRIPT'
#!/bin/bash
URL="https://backend.appmiaoda.com/projects/supabase318302677194813440/auth/v1/admin/users"
KEY="eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiIsInR5cCI6IkpXVCJ9.eyJhdWQiOiJhdXRoZW50aWNhdGVkIiwiZXhwIjoyMDk1MzE2NDcyLCJpc3MiOiJzdXBhYmFzZSIsInJvbGUiOiJzZXJ2aWNlX3JvbGUiLCJzdWIiOiJzZXJ2aWNlX3JvbGUifQ.wa5S6YQ2FzQHDg8D_DhwJ2Nd7CTv6gqrOL-K2oUgYUI"

success=0
failed=0

# 创建2个管理账户
for u in admin1 admin2; do
  res=$(curl -s -X POST "$URL" \
    -H "apikey: $KEY" -H "Authorization: Bearer $KEY" \
    -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
    -d "{\"email\":\"${u}@miaoda.com\",\"password\":\"Admin@1234\",\"email_confirm\":true,\"user_metadata\":{\"display_name\":\"${u}\",\"role\":\"admin\"}}")
  if echo "$res" | grep -q '"id"'; then
    echo "✅ $u 创建成功"
    ((success++))
  else
    echo "❌ $u 创建失败: $res"
    ((failed++))
  fi
  sleep 0.3
done

# 创建30个普通账户 (reviewer)
for i in $(seq -w 1 30); do
  u="member${i}"
  res=$(curl -s -X POST "$URL" \
    -H "apikey: $KEY" -H "Authorization: Bearer $KEY" \
    -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
    -d "{\"email\":\"${u}@miaoda.com\",\"password\":\"Member@1234\",\"email_confirm\":true,\"user_metadata\":{\"display_name\":\"成员${i}\",\"role\":\"reviewer\"}}")
  if echo "$res" | grep -q '"id"'; then
    echo "✅ $u 创建成功"
    ((success++))
  else
    echo "❌ $u 创建失败: $res"
    ((failed++))
  fi
  sleep 0.3
done

echo ""
echo "总计: 成功 $success, 失败 $failed"
SCRIPT
chmod +x /tmp/create_users.sh && /tmp/create_users.sh
</action>

PB 里没有这个函数，也不能直接建同名 RPC

     1	import { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
     2	import { supabase } from '@/db/supabase';
     3	import type { ReviewCycle } from '@/types/types';
     4	
     5	/**
     6	 * 自动确保近 `monthsBack` 个自然月的周期存在，并返回列表。
     7	 * 默认显示近 3 个月，按月份倒序排列（最新在前）。
     8	 */
     9	export function useMonthCycles(monthsBack = 3) {
    10	  const [cycles, setCycles] = useState<ReviewCycle[]>([]);
    11	  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
    12	  const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null);
    13	
    14	  useEffect(() => {
    15	    let cancelled = false;
    16	    const run = async () => {
    17	      setLoading(true);
    18	      setError(null);
    19	      const { data, error: rpcError } = await supabase.rpc('ensure_month_cycles', {
    20	        months_back: monthsBack,
    21	      });
    22	      if (!cancelled) {
    23	        if (rpcError) {
    24	          setError(rpcError.message);
    25	          console.error('useMonthCycles RPC 失败:', rpcError.message);
    26	        } else if (Array.isArray(data)) {
    27	          // 按 year_month 倒序确保顺序一致
    28	          const sorted = [...data].sort((a, b) =>
    29	            (b.year_month ?? '').localeCompare(a.year_month ?? '')
    30	          );
    31	          setCycles(sorted as ReviewCycle[]);
    32	        }
    33	        setLoading(false);
    34	      }
    35	    };
    36	    run();
    37	    return () => { cancelled = true; };
    38	  }, [monthsBack]);
    39	
    40	  /** 当前月（列表第一项） */
    41	  const currentCycle = cycles[0] ?? null;
    42	
    43	  return { cycles, loading, error, currentCycle };
    44	}

     9	export async function getProfile(userId: string): Promise<Profile | null> {
    10	  const { data, error } = await supabase
    11	    .from('profiles')
    12	    .select('*')
    13	    .eq('id', userId)
    14	    .maybeSingle();
    15

    17	    console.error('获取用户信息失败:', error);
    18	    return null;
    19	  }
    20	  return data;
    21	}
    22	interface AuthContextType {
    23	  user: User | null;
    24	  profile: Profile | null;

    40	    if (!user) {
    41	      setProfile(null);
    42	      return;
    43	    }
    44	
    45	    const profileData = await getProfile(user.id);
    46	    setProfile(profileData);
    47	  };
    48	
    49	  useEffect(() => {
    50	    supabase
    51	      .auth
    52	      .getSession()
    53	      // @ts-ignore
    54	      .then(({ data: { session } }) => {
    55	        setUser(session?.user ?? null);
    56	        if (session?.user) {
    57	          getProfile(session.user.id).then(setProfile);
    58	        }
    59	      })

     2	import { supabase } from '@/db/supabase';

    10	import { useMonthCycles } from '@/hooks/use-month-cycles';
    11	import type { ReviewCycle } from '@/types/types';
    12	
    13	export default function CycleManagementPage() {
    14	  const { cycles, loading, currentCycle } = useMonthCycles(3);
    15	  const [toggling, setToggling] = useState<string | null>(null);
    16	  // 乐观更新状态：key 为 cycle.id，value 为覆盖的 is_active 值
    17	  const [overrides, setOverrides] = useState<Record<string, boolean>>({});
    18	
    19	  // 将 hook 数据与本地乐观覆盖合并，保持同步
    20	  const displayed: ReviewCycle[] = cycles.map((c) =>
    21	    c.id in overrides ? { ...c, is_active: overrides[c.id] } : c
    22	  );
    23	
    24	  const handleToggleActive = useCallback(async (cycle: ReviewCycle) => {
    25	    const currentActive = overrides[cycle.id] ?? cycle.is_active;
    26	    const next = !currentActive;
    27	    setToggling(cycle.id);
    28	    // 乐观更新
    29	    setOverrides((prev) => ({ ...prev, [cycle.id]: next }));
    30	    const { error } = await supabase
    31	      .from('review_cycles')
    32	      .update({ is_active: next })
    33	      .eq('id', cycle.id);
    34	    setToggling(null);
    35	    if (error) {
    36	      // 回滚
    37	      setOverrides((prev) => ({ ...prev, [cycle.id]: currentActive }));
    38	      toast.error('操作失败');
    39	    } else {
    40	      toast.success(next ? `「${cycle.name}」已开启评价` : `「${cycle.name}」已关闭评价`);
    41	    }
    42	  }, [overrides]);
    43	
    44	  return (
    45	    <div className="max-w-3xl mx-auto space-y-6">
    46	      {/* 页头 */}
    47	      <div className="flex items-start justify-between gap-3">
    48	        <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
    49	          <Calendar className="w-5 h-5 text-primary shrink-0" />
    50	          <div>
    51	            <h1 className="text-xl font-semibold text-balance">评价周期</h1>
    52	            <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground text-pretty">
    53	              周期按自然月自动生成，默认显示近 3 个月。开启后成员可在该月填写评价。
    54	            </p>
    55	          </div>
    56	        </div>
    57	      </div>
    58	
    59	      {/* 当前月提示卡 */}
    60	      {currentCycle && (
    61	        <Card className="shadow-card border-primary/20 bg-primary/5">
    62	          <CardContent className="py-4 flex items-center gap-3">
    63	            <div className="w-9 h-9 rounded-full bg-primary/10 flex items-center justify-center shrink-0">
    64	              <Calendar className="w-4 h-4 text-primary" />
    65	            </div>
    66	            <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
    67	              <p className="text-sm font-semibold">当前自然月：{currentCycle.name}</p>
    68	              <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">
    69	                {currentCycle.start_date} — {currentCycle.end_date}
    70	                {currentCycle.is_active
    71	                  ? '  ·  评价填写中'
    72	                  : '  ·  已关闭（可手动开启）'}
    73	              </p>
    74	            </div>
    75	            <Badge variant={currentCycle.is_active ? 'default' : 'secondary'} className="shrink-0">
    76	              {currentCycle.is_active ? '进行中' : '已关闭'}
    77	            </Badge>
    78	          </CardContent>
    79	        </Card>
    80	      )}
    81	
    82	      {/* 近3个月列表 */}
    83	      <Card className="shadow-card">
    84	        <CardHeader className="pb-3">
    85	          <CardTitle className="text-base flex items-center gap-2">
    86	            <RefreshCw className="w-4 h-4 text-muted-foreground" />
    87	            近 3 个月概览
    88	          </CardTitle>
    89	        </CardHeader>
    90	        <CardContent className="p-0">
    91	          {loading ? (
    92	            <div className="p-4 space-y-3">
    93	              {Array.from({ length: 3 }).map((_, i) => (
    94	                <Skeleton key={i} className="h-16 w-full bg-muted" />
    95	              ))}
    96	            </div>
    97	          ) : (
    98	            <div className="divide-y divide-border">
    99	              {displayed.map((cycle) => {
   100	                const isToggling = toggling === cycle.id;
   101	                const isCurrentMonth = cycle.year_month === currentCycle?.year_month;
   102	                return (
   103	                  <div
   104	                    key={cycle.id}
   105	                    className="px-4 py-4 flex items-center gap-4 hover:bg-muted/20 transition-colors"
   106	                  >
   107	                    {/* 月份标签 */}
   108	                    <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
   109	                      <div className="flex items-center gap-2 flex-wrap">
   110	                        <span className="text-sm font-semibold">{cycle.name}</span>
   111	                        {isCurrentMonth && (
   112	                          <Badge variant="outline" className="text-[10px] py-0 border-primary text-primary">
   113	                            本月
   114	                          </Badge>
   115	                        )}
   116	                      </div>
   117	                      <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground mt-0.5">
   118	                        {cycle.start_date} — {cycle.end_date}
   119	                      </p>
   120	                    </div>
   121	
   122	                    {/* 状态 */}
   123	                    <div className="flex items-center gap-2 shrink-0">

   125	                        variant={cycle.is_active ? 'default' : 'secondary'}
   126	                        className="text-xs gap-1"
   127	                      >
   128	                        {cycle.is_active ? (
   129	                          <><CheckCircle className="w-3 h-3" />开放填写</>

   138	                      />
   139	                    </div>
   140	                  </div>
   141	                );
   142	              })}
   143	            </div>

   153	      </div>

     1	import { createContext, useContext, useEffect, useState, type ReactNode } from 'react';
     2	// @ts-ignore
     3	import { supabase } from '@/db/supabase';
     4	import type { User } from '@supabase/supabase-js';
     5	// @ts-ignore
     6	import type { Profile } from '@/types/types';
     7	import { toast } from 'sonner';
     8	
     9	export async function getProfile(userId: string): Promise<Profile | null> {
    10	  const { data, error } = await supabase
    11	    .from('profiles')
    12	    .select('*')
    13	    .eq('id', userId)
    14	    .maybeSingle();
    15	
    16	  if (error) {
    17	    console.error('获取用户信息失败:', error);
    18	    return null;
    19	  }
    20	  return data;
    21	}
    22	interface AuthContextType {
    23	  user: User | null;
    24	  profile: Profile | null;
    25	  loading: boolean;
    26	  signInWithUsername: (username: string, password: string) => Promise<{ error: Error | null }>;
    27	  signUpWithUsername: (username: string, password: string) => Promise<{ error: Error | null }>;
    28	  signOut: () => Promise<void>;
    29	  refreshProfile: () => Promise<void>;
    30	}
    31	
    32	const AuthContext = createContext<AuthContextType | undefined>(undefined);
    33	
    34	export function AuthProvider({ children }: { children: ReactNode }) {
    35	  const [user, setUser] = useState<User | null>(null);
    36	  const [profile, setProfile] = useState<Profile | null>(null);
    37	  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
    38	
    39	  const refreshProfile = async () => {
    40	    if (!user) {
    41	      setProfile(null);
    42	      return;
    43	    }
    44	
    45	    const profileData = await getProfile(user.id);
    46	    setProfile(profileData);
    47	  };
    48	
    49	  useEffect(() => {
    50	    supabase
    51	      .auth
    52	      .getSession()
    53	      // @ts-ignore
    54	      .then(({ data: { session } }) => {
    55	        setUser(session?.user ?? null);
    56	        if (session?.user) {
    57	          getProfile(session.user.id).then(setProfile);
    58	        }
    59	      })
    60	      // @ts-ignore
    61	      .catch(error => {
    62	        toast.error(`获取用户信息失败: ${error.message}`);
    63	      })
    64	      .finally(() => {
    65	        setLoading(false);
    66	      });
    67	
    68	    // @ts-ignore
    69	    // In this function, do NOT use any await calls. Use `.then()` instead to avoid deadlocks.
    70	    const { data: { subscription } } = supabase.auth.onAuthStateChange((_event, session) => {
    71	      setUser(session?.user ?? null);
    72	      if (session?.user) {
    73	        getProfile(session.user.id).then(setProfile);
    74	      } else {
    75	        setProfile(null);
    76	      }
    77	    });
    78	
    79	    return () => subscription.unsubscribe();
    80	  }, []);
    81	
    82	  const signInWithUsername = async (username: string, password: string) => {
    83	    try {
    84	      const email = `${username}@miaoda.com`;
    85	      const { error } = await supabase.auth.signInWithPassword({
    86	        email,
    87	        password,
    88	      });
    89	
    90	      if (error) throw error;
    91	      return { error: null };
    92	    } catch (error) {
    93	      return { error: error as Error };
    94	    }
    95	  };
    96	
    97	  const signUpWithUsername = async (username: string, password: string) => {
    98	    try {
    99	      const email = `${username}@miaoda.com`;
   100	      const { error } = await supabase.auth.signUp({
   101	        email,
   102	        password,
   103	      });
   104	
   105	      if (error) throw error;
   106	      return { error: null };
   107	    } catch (error) {
   108	      return { error: error as Error };
   109	    }
   110	  };
   111	
   112	  const signOut = async () => {
   113	    await supabase.auth.signOut();
   114	    setUser(null);
   115	    setProfile(null);
   116	  };
   117	
   118	  return (
   119	    <AuthContext.Provider value={{ user, profile, loading, signInWithUsername, signUpWithUsername, signOut, refreshProfile }}>
   120	      {children}
   121	    </AuthContext.Provider>
   122	  );
   123	}
   124	
   125	export function useAuth() {
   126	  const context = useContext(AuthContext);
   127	  if (context === undefined) {
   128	    throw new Error('useAuth must be used within an AuthProvider');
   129	  }
   130	  return context;
   131	}

     1	import { useState, useEffect, useCallback } from 'react';

Command: str_replace
Old String: ```
import { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import { supabase } from '@/db/supabase';
import type { ReviewCycle } from '@/types/types';

/**
 * 自动确保近 `monthsBack` 个自然月的周期存在，并返回列表。
 * 默认显示近 3 个月，按月份倒序排列（最新在前）。
 */
export function useMonthCycles(monthsBack = 3) {
  const [cycles, setCycles] = useState<ReviewCycle[]>([]);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
  const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null);

  useEffect(() => {
    let cancelled = false;
    const run = async () => {
      setLoading(true);
      setError(null);
      const { data, error: rpcError } = await supabase.rpc('ensure_month_cycles', {
        months_back: monthsBack,
      });
      if (!cancelled) {
        if (rpcError) {
          setError(rpcError.message);
          console.error('useMonthCycles RPC 失败:', rpcError.message);
        } else if (Array.isArray(data)) {
          // 按 year_month 倒序确保顺序一致
          const sorted = [...data].sort((a, b) =>
            (b.year_month ?? '').localeCompare(a.year_month ?? '')
          );
          setCycles(sorted as ReviewCycle[]);
        }
        setLoading(false);
      }
    };
    run();
    return () => { cancelled = true; };
  }, [monthsBack]);

  /** 当前月（列表第一项） */
  const currentCycle = cycles[0] ?? null;

  return { cycles, loading, error, currentCycle };
}
```
New String: ```
import { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import { pb } from '@/db/pb';
import type { ReviewCycle } from '@/types/types';

/** 生成近 N 个自然月的 YYYY-MM 字符串，最新在前 */
function getMonthKeys(monthsBack: number): string[] {
  const keys: string[] = [];
  const now = new Date();
  for (let i = 0; i < monthsBack; i++) {
    const d = new Date(now.getFullYear(), now.getMonth() - i, 1);
    const y = d.getFullYear();
    const m = String(d.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0');
    keys.push(`${y}-${m}`);
  }
  return keys; // 已按倒序排列（最新在前）
}

/** 获取某月最后一天的日期字符串 YYYY-MM-DD */
function lastDayOf(yearMonth: string): string {
  const [y, m] = yearMonth.split('-').map(Number);
  const last = new Date(y, m, 0); // 下月第0天 = 当月最后一天
  const mm = String(last.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0');
  const dd = String(last.getDate()).padStart(2, '0');
  return `${last.getFullYear()}-${mm}-${dd}`;
}

/**
 * 自动确保近 `monthsBack` 个自然月的周期存在，并返回列表。
 * 替代原 Supabase RPC ensure_month_cycles，改用 PocketBase 标准 API。
 * 默认显示近 3 个月，按月份倒序排列（最新在前）。
 */
export function useMonthCycles(monthsBack = 3) {
  const [cycles, setCycles] = useState<ReviewCycle[]>([]);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
  const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null);

  useEffect(() => {
    let cancelled = false;
    const run = async () => {
      setLoading(true);
      setError(null);
      try {
        const monthKeys = getMonthKeys(monthsBack);
        const currentMonthKey = monthKeys[0]; // 最新的一个月

        // 1. 查询已存在的周期（过滤近 N 个月）
        const filterExpr = monthKeys.map(k => `year_month="${k}"`).join('||');
        const existingResult = await pb.collection('review_cycles').getList<ReviewCycle>(1, 50, {
          filter: filterExpr,
          sort: '-year_month',
        });
        const existing = existingResult.items;
        const existingKeys = new Set(existing.map(c => c.year_month));

        // 2. 补全缺失的月份
        const toCreate = monthKeys.filter(k => !existingKeys.has(k));
        const created: ReviewCycle[] = [];
        for (const key of toCreate) {
          const [y, m] = key.split('-');
          const name = `${y}年${parseInt(m)}月`;
          const startDate = `${key}-01`;
          const endDate = lastDayOf(key);
          const isActive = key === currentMonthKey; // 当前月默认开启
          const record = await pb.collection('review_cycles').create<ReviewCycle>({
            name,
            start_date: startDate,
            end_date: endDate,
            is_active: isActive,
            year_month: key,
          });
          created.push(record);
        }

        // 3. 合并并按 year_month 倒序排列
        const all = [...existing, ...created].sort((a, b) =>
          (b.year_month ?? '').localeCompare(a.year_month ?? '')
        );

        if (!cancelled) {
          setCycles(all);
          setLoading(false);
        }
      } catch (err) {
        if (!cancelled) {
          const msg = err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err);
          setError(msg);
          console.error('useMonthCycles 失败:', msg);
          setLoading(false);
        }
      }
    };
    run();
    return () => { cancelled = true; };
  }, [monthsBack]);

  /** 当前月（列表第一项） */
  const currentCycle = cycles[0] ?? null;

  return { cycles, loading, error, currentCycle };
}
```

     1	import { createContext, useContext, useEffect, useState, type ReactNode } from 'react';
     2	// @ts-ignore
     3	import { supabase } from '@/db/supabase';
     4	import type { User } from '@supabase/supabase-js';
     5	// @ts-ignore
     6	import type { Profile } from '@/types/types';
     7	import { toast } from 'sonner';
     8	
     9	export async function getProfile(userId: string): Promise<Profile | null> {
    10	  const { data, error } = await supabase
    11	    .from('profiles')
    12	    .select('*')
    13	    .eq('id', userId)
    14	    .maybeSingle();
    15	
    16	  if (error) {
    17	    console.error('获取用户信息失败:', error);
    18	    return null;
    19	  }
    20	  return data;
    21	}
    22	interface AuthContextType {
    23	  user: User | null;
    24	  profile: Profile | null;
    25	  loading: boolean;
    26	  signInWithUsername: (username: string, password: string) => Promise<{ error: Error | null }>;
    27	  signUpWithUsername: (username: string, password: string) => Promise<{ error: Error | null }>;
    28	  signOut: () => Promise<void>;
    29	  refreshProfile: () => Promise<void>;
    30	}
    31	
    32	const AuthContext = createContext<AuthContextType | undefined>(undefined);
    33	
    34	export function AuthProvider({ children }: { children: ReactNode }) {
    35	  const [user, setUser] = useState<User | null>(null);
    36	  const [profile, setProfile] = useState<Profile | null>(null);
    37	  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
    38	
    39	  const refreshProfile = async () => {
    40	    if (!user) {
    41	      setProfile(null);
    42	      return;
    43	    }
    44	
    45	    const profileData = await getProfile(user.id);
    46	    setProfile(profileData);
    47	  };
    48	
    49	  useEffect(() => {
    50	    supabase
    51	      .auth
    52	      .getSession()
    53	      // @ts-ignore
    54	      .then(({ data: { session } }) => {
    55	        setUser(session?.user ?? null);
    56	        if (session?.user) {
    57	          getProfile(session.user.id).then(setProfile);
    58	        }
    59	      })
    60	      // @ts-ignore
    61	      .catch(error => {
    62	        toast.error(`获取用户信息失败: ${error.message}`);
    63	      })
    64	      .finally(() => {
    65	        setLoading(false);
    66	      });
    67	
    68	    // @ts-ignore
    69	    // In this function, do NOT use any await calls. Use `.then()` instead to avoid deadlocks.
    70	    const { data: { subscription } } = supabase.auth.onAuthStateChange((_event, session) => {
    71	      setUser(session?.user ?? null);
    72	      if (session?.user) {
    73	        getProfile(session.user.id).then(setProfile);
    74	      } else {
    75	        setProfile(null);
    76	      }
    77	    });
    78	
    79	    return () => subscription.unsubscribe();
    80	  }, []);
    81	
    82	  const signInWithUsername = async (username: string, password: string) => {
    83	    try {
    84	      const email = `${username}@miaoda.com`;
    85	      const { error } = await supabase.auth.signInWithPassword({
    86	        email,
    87	        password,
    88	      });
    89	
    90	      if (error) throw error;
    91	      return { error: null };
    92	    } catch (error) {
    93	      return { error: error as Error };
    94	    }
    95	  };
    96	
    97	  const signUpWithUsername = async (username: string, password: string) => {
    98	    try {
    99	      const email = `${username}@miaoda.com`;
   100	      const { error } = await supabase.auth.signUp({
   101	        email,
   102	        password,
   103	      });
   104	
   105	      if (error) throw error;
   106	      return { error: null };
   107	    } catch (error) {
   108	      return { error: error as Error };
   109	    }
   110	  };
   111	
   112	  const signOut = async () => {
   113	    await supabase.auth.signOut();
   114	    setUser(null);
   115	    setProfile(null);
   116	  };
   117	
   118	  return (
   119	    <AuthContext.Provider value={{ user, profile, loading, signInWithUsername, signUpWithUsername, signOut, refreshProfile }}>
   120	      {children}
   121	    </AuthContext.Provider>
   122	  );
   123	}
   124	
   125	export function useAuth() {
   126	  const context = useContext(AuthContext);
   127	  if (context === undefined) {
   128	    throw new Error('useAuth must be used within an AuthProvider');
   129	  }
   130	  return context;
   131	}

     1	import { cn } from '@/lib/utils'
     2	import { type UseSupabaseUploadReturn } from '@/hooks/use-supabase-upload'
     3	import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button'
     4	import { CheckCircle, File, Loader2, Upload, X } from 'lucide-react'
     5	import { createContext, type PropsWithChildren, useCallback, useContext } from 'react'
     6	
     7	export const formatBytes = (
     8	  bytes: number,
     9	  decimals = 2,
    10	  size?: 'bytes' | 'KB' | 'MB' | 'GB' | 'TB' | 'PB' | 'EB' | 'ZB' | 'YB'
    11	) => {
    12	  const k = 1000
    13	  const dm = decimals < 0 ? 0 : decimals
    14	  const sizes = ['bytes', 'KB', 'MB', 'GB', 'TB', 'PB', 'EB', 'ZB', 'YB']
    15	
    16	  if (bytes === 0 || bytes === undefined) return size !== undefined ? `0 ${size}` : '0 bytes'
    17	  const i = size !== undefined ? sizes.indexOf(size) : Math.floor(Math.log(bytes) / Math.log(k))
    18	  return parseFloat((bytes / Math.pow(k, i)).toFixed(dm)) + ' ' + sizes[i]
    19	}
    20	
    21	type DropzoneContextType = Omit<UseSupabaseUploadReturn, 'getRootProps' | 'getInputProps'>
    22	
    23	const DropzoneContext = createContext<DropzoneContextType | undefined>(undefined)
    24	
    25	type DropzoneProps = UseSupabaseUploadReturn & {
    26	  className?: string
    27	}
    28	
    29	const Dropzone = ({
    30	  className,
    31	  children,
    32	  getRootProps,
    33	  getInputProps,
    34	  ...restProps
    35	}: PropsWithChildren<DropzoneProps>) => {
    36	  const isSuccess = restProps.isSuccess
    37	  const isActive = restProps.isDragActive
    38	  const isInvalid =
    39	    (restProps.isDragActive && restProps.isDragReject) ||
    40	    (restProps.errors.length > 0 && !restProps.isSuccess) ||
    41	    restProps.files.some((file) => file.errors.length !== 0)
    42	
    43	  return (
    44	    <DropzoneContext.Provider value={{ ...restProps }}>
    45	      <div
    46	        {...getRootProps({
    47	          className: cn(
    48	            'border-2 border-gray-300 rounded-lg p-6 text-center bg-card transition-colors duration-300 text-foreground',
    49	            className,
    50	            isSuccess ? 'border-solid' : 'border-dashed',
    51	            isActive && 'border-primary bg-primary/10',
    52	            isInvalid && 'border-destructive bg-destructive/10'
    53	          ),
    54	        })}
    55	      >
    56	        <input {...getInputProps()} />
    57	        {children}
    58	      </div>
    59	    </DropzoneContext.Provider>
    60	  )
    61	}
    62	const DropzoneContent = ({ className }: { className?: string }) => {
    63	  const {
    64	    files,
    65	    setFiles,
    66	    onUpload,
    67	    loading,
    68	    successes,
    69	    errors,
    70	    maxFileSize,
    71	    maxFiles,
    72	    isSuccess,
    73	  } = useDropzoneContext()
    74	
    75	  const exceedMaxFiles = files.length > maxFiles
    76	
    77	  const handleRemoveFile = useCallback(
    78	    (fileName: string) => {
    79	      setFiles(files.filter((file) => file.name !== fileName))
    80	    },
    81	    [files, setFiles]
    82	  )
    83	
    84	  if (isSuccess) {
    85	    return (
    86	      <div className={cn('flex flex-row items-center gap-x-2 justify-center', className)}>
    87	        <CheckCircle size={16} className="text-primary" />
    88	        <p className="text-primary text-sm">
    89	          Successfully uploaded {files.length} file{files.length > 1 ? 's' : ''}
    90	        </p>
    91	      </div>
    92	    )
    93	  }
    94	
    95	  return (
    96	    <div className={cn('flex flex-col', className)}>
    97	      {files.map((file, idx) => {
    98	        const fileError = errors.find((e) => e.name === file.name)
    99	        const isSuccessfullyUploaded = !!successes.find((e) => e === file.name)
   100	
   101	        return (
   102	          <div
   103	            key={`${file.name}-${idx}`}
   104	            className="flex items-center gap-x-4 border-b py-2 first:mt-4 last:mb-4 "
   105	          >
   106	            {file.type.startsWith('image/') ? (
   107	              <div className="h-10 w-10 rounded border overflow-hidden shrink-0 bg-muted flex items-center justify-center">
   108	                <img src={file.preview} alt={file.name} className="object-cover" />
   109	              </div>
   110	            ) : (
   111	              <div className="h-10 w-10 rounded border bg-muted flex items-center justify-center">
   112	                <File size={18} />
   113	              </div>
   114	            )}
   115	
   116	            <div className="shrink grow flex flex-col items-start truncate">
   117	              <p title={file.name} className="text-sm truncate max-w-full">
   118	                {file.name}
   119	              </p>
   120	              {file.errors.length > 0 ? (
   121	                <p className="text-xs text-destructive">
   122	                  {file.errors
   123	                    .map((e) =>
   124	                      e.message.startsWith('File is larger than')
   125	                        ? `File is larger than ${formatBytes(maxFileSize, 2)} (Size: ${formatBytes(file.size, 2)})`
   126	                        : e.message
   127	                    )
   128	                    .join(', ')}
   129	                </p>
   130	              ) : loading && !isSuccessfullyUploaded ? (
   131	                <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">Uploading file...</p>
   132	              ) : !!fileError ? (
   133	                <p className="text-xs text-destructive">Failed to upload: {fileError.message}</p>
   134	              ) : isSuccessfullyUploaded ? (
   135	                <p className="text-xs text-primary">Successfully uploaded file</p>
   136	              ) : (
   137	                <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">{formatBytes(file.size, 2)}</p>
   138	              )}
   139	            </div>
   140	
   141	            {!loading && !isSuccessfullyUploaded && (
   142	              <Button
   143	                size="icon"
   144	                variant="link"
   145	                className="shrink-0 justify-self-end text-muted-foreground hover:text-foreground"
   146	                onClick={() => handleRemoveFile(file.name)}
   147	              >
   148	                <X />
   149	              </Button>
   150	            )}
   151	          </div>
   152	        )
   153	      })}
   154	      {exceedMaxFiles && (
   155	        <p className="text-sm text-left mt-2 text-destructive">
   156	          You may upload only up to {maxFiles} files, please remove {files.length - maxFiles} file
   157	          {files.length - maxFiles > 1 ? 's' : ''}.
   158	        </p>
   159	      )}
   160	      {files.length > 0 && !exceedMaxFiles && (
   161	        <div className="mt-2">
   162	          <Button
   163	            variant="outline"
   164	            onClick={onUpload}
   165	            disabled={files.some((file) => file.errors.length !== 0) || loading}
   166	          >
   167	            {loading ? (
   168	              <>
   169	                <Loader2 className="mr-2 h-4 w-4 animate-spin" />
   170	                Uploading...
   171	              </>
   172	            ) : (
   173	              <>Upload files</>
   174	            )}
   175	          </Button>
   176	        </div>
   177	      )}
   178	    </div>
   179	  )
   180	}
   181	
   182	const DropzoneEmptyState = ({ className }: { className?: string }) => {
   183	  const { maxFiles, maxFileSize, inputRef, isSuccess } = useDropzoneContext()
   184	
   185	  if (isSuccess) {
   186	    return null
   187	  }
   188	
   189	  return (
   190	    <div className={cn('flex flex-col items-center gap-y-2', className)}>
   191	      <Upload size={20} className="text-muted-foreground" />
   192	      <p className="text-sm">
   193	        Upload{!!maxFiles && maxFiles > 1 ? ` ${maxFiles}` : ''} file
   194	        {!maxFiles || maxFiles > 1 ? 's' : ''}
   195	      </p>
   196	      <div className="flex flex-col items-center gap-y-1">
   197	        <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">
   198	          Drag and drop or{' '}
   199	          <a
   200	            onClick={() => inputRef.current?.click()}
   201	            className="underline cursor-pointer transition hover:text-foreground"
   202	          >
   203	            select {maxFiles === 1 ? `file` : 'files'}
   204	          </a>{' '}
   205	          to upload
   206	        </p>
   207	        {maxFileSize !== Number.POSITIVE_INFINITY && (
   208	          <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">
   209	            Maximum file size: {formatBytes(maxFileSize, 2)}
   210	          </p>
   211	        )}
   212	      </div>
   213	    </div>
   214	  )
   215	}
   216	
   217	const useDropzoneContext = () => {
   218	  const context = useContext(DropzoneContext)
   219	
   220	  if (!context) {
   221	    throw new Error('useDropzoneContext must be used within a Dropzone')
   222	  }
   223	
   224	  return context
   225	}
   226	
   227	export { Dropzone, DropzoneContent, DropzoneEmptyState, useDropzoneContext }

    19	// 星级评分组件
    20	function StarRating({
    21	  value,
    22	  onChange,
    23	  disabled,
    24	}: {
    25	  value: number | null;
    26	  onChange: (v: number) => void;
    27	  disabled?: boolean;
    28	}) {
    29	  const [hovered, setHovered] = useState<number | null>(null);
    30	  return (
    31	    <div className="flex items-center gap-0.5">
    32	      {[1, 2, 3, 4, 5].map((star) => {
    33	        const active = (hovered ?? value ?? 0) >= star;
    34	        return (
    35	          <button
    36	            key={star}
    37	            type="button"
    38	            disabled={disabled}
    39	            className={`p-0.5 transition-colors ${disabled ? 'cursor-not-allowed opacity-60' : 'cursor-pointer'}`}
    40	            onMouseEnter={() => !disabled && setHovered(star)}
    41	            onMouseLeave={() => !disabled && setHovered(null)}
    42	            onClick={() => !disabled && onChange(star)}
    43	          >
    44	            <Star
    45	              className={`w-5 h-5 transition-colors ${
    46	                active ? 'text-yellow-400 fill-yellow-400' : 'text-muted-foreground'
    47	              }`}
    48	            />
    49	          </button>
    50	        );
    51	      })}
    52	      {value !== null && (
    53	        <span className="text-xs text-muted-foreground ml-1">{value} 分</span>
    54	      )}
    55	    </div>
    56	  );
    57	}

    59	const emptyForm = (): ReviewFormData =>
    60	  Object.fromEntries(
    61	    DIMENSIONS.map((d) => [d, { score: null, note: '' }])
    62	  ) as ReviewFormData;

    64	// 多选人员下拉组件
    65	function PeoplePicker({
    66	  reviewees,
    67	  submitted,
    68	  selected,
    69	  onToggle,
    70	  onSelectAllPending,
    71	  onClearAll,
    72	}: {
    73	  reviewees: Profile[];
    74	  submitted: Set<string>;
    75	  selected: Set<string>;
    76	  onToggle: (id: string) => void;
    77	  onSelectAllPending: () => void;
    78	  onClearAll: () => void;
    79	}) {
    80	  const [open, setOpen] = useState(false);
    81	  const pending = reviewees.filter((u) => !submitted.has(u.id));
    82	  const selectedPending = [...selected].filter((id) => !submitted.has(id));
    83	
    84	  const triggerLabel = () => {
    85	    if (selected.size === 0) return '请选择评价对象';
    86	    return `已选 ${selected.size} 人`;
    87	  };
    88	
    89	  return (
    90	    <Popover open={open} onOpenChange={setOpen}>
    91	      <PopoverTrigger asChild>
    92	        <Button
    93	          variant="outline"
    94	          className="w-full md:w-72 justify-between font-normal"
    95	        >
    96	          <span className="flex items-center gap-2 min-w-0">
    97	            <Users className="w-4 h-4 shrink-0 text-muted-foreground" />
    98	            <span className="truncate">{triggerLabel()}</span>
    99	          </span>
   100	          <ChevronDown className="w-4 h-4 shrink-0 text-muted-foreground ml-2" />
   101	        </Button>
   102	      </PopoverTrigger>
   103	      <PopoverContent
   104	        className="w-72 p-0"
   105	        align="start"
   106	        sideOffset={4}
   107	      >
   108	        {/* 快捷操作 */}
   109	        <div className="flex items-center justify-between px-3 py-2 border-b border-border">
   110	          <button
   111	            className="text-xs text-primary hover:underline disabled:opacity-40 disabled:no-underline"
   112	            onClick={onSelectAllPending}
   113	            disabled={pending.length === 0 || selectedPending.length === pending.length}
   114	          >
   115	            全选待评（{pending.length}）
   116	          </button>
   117	          <button
   118	            className="text-xs text-muted-foreground hover:text-foreground disabled:opacity-40"
   119	            onClick={onClearAll}
   120	            disabled={selected.size === 0}
   121	          >
   122	            <X className="w-3.5 h-3.5" />
   123	          </button>
   124	        </div>
   125	
   126	        {/* 成员列表 */}
   127	        <div className="max-h-60 overflow-y-auto py-1">
   128	          {reviewees.length === 0 ? (
   129	            <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground text-center py-4">暂无其他成员</p>
   130	          ) : (
   131	            reviewees.map((u) => {
   132	              const isSubmitted = submitted.has(u.id);
   133	              const isChecked = selected.has(u.id) || isSubmitted;
   134	              return (
   135	                <label
   136	                  key={u.id}
   137	                  className={`flex items-center gap-3 px-3 py-2 cursor-pointer hover:bg-muted/40 transition-colors ${
   138	                    isSubmitted ? 'opacity-50 cursor-not-allowed' : ''
   139	                  }`}
   140	                >
   141	                  <Checkbox
   142	                    checked={isChecked}
   143	                    disabled={isSubmitted}
   144	                    onCheckedChange={() => !isSubmitted && onToggle(u.id)}
   145	                  />
   146	                  <div className="w-7 h-7 rounded-full bg-primary/10 flex items-center justify-center text-xs font-bold text-primary shrink-0">
   147	                    {(u.display_name || u.username)[0].toUpperCase()}
   148	                  </div>
   149	                  <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
   150	                    <p className="text-sm truncate">{u.display_name || u.username}</p>
   151	                    <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground truncate">@{u.username}</p>
   152	                  </div>
   153	                  {isSubmitted && (
   154	                    <CheckCircle className="w-3.5 h-3.5 text-green-600 shrink-0" />
   155	                  )}
   156	                </label>
   157	              );
   158	            })
   159	          )}
   160	        </div>
   161	
   162	        {/* 底部关闭 */}
   163	        {selected.size > 0 && (
   164	          <div className="border-t border-border px-3 py-2">
   165	            <Button size="sm" className="w-full h-8" onClick={() => setOpen(false)}>
   166	              确认（{selected.size} 人）
   167	            </Button>
   168	          </div>
   169	        )}
   170	      </PopoverContent>
   171	    </Popover>
   172	  );
   173	}

   187

   191	  const [submitting, setSubmitting] = useState<string | null>(null);
   192	  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);
   193	  // 多选：当前选中待评价的人员
   194	  const [selectedPeople, setSelectedPeople] = useState<Set<string>>(new Set());
   195	
   196	  const selectedCycleInfo = cycles.find((c) => c.id === selectedCycle);
   197

   200	    setLoading(true);
   201	    const { data: profiles } = await supabase
   202	      .from('profiles')
   203	      .select('id, username, display_name, role, created_at')
   204	      .neq('id', profile.id)
   205	      .order('display_name');
   206	
   207	    const { data: myReviews } = await supabase
   208	      .from('reviews')
   209	      .select('reviewee_id')
   210	      .eq('cycle_id', selectedCycle)
   211	      .eq('reviewer_id', profile.id);
   212

   217	    setReviewees(users);
   218	    setSubmitted(submittedSet);
   219	    setSelectedPeople(new Set()); // 切换月份时清空选择
   220	
   221	    const init: Record<string, ReviewFormData> = {};
   222	    for (const u of users) {
   223	      init[u.id] = emptyForm();
   224	    }
   225	    setFormMap(init);
   226	    setLoading(false);
   227	  }, [selectedCycle, profile]);
   228	
   229	  useEffect(() => {
   230	    fetchRevieweesAndStatus();
   231	  }, [fetchRevieweesAndStatus]);
   232	
   233	  const togglePerson = (id: string) => {

   236	      if (next.has(id)) next.delete(id);

   241

   355	                {!canSubmit && (
   356

     1	import { useState, useEffect, useCallback } from 'react';
     2	import { supabase } from '@/db/supabase';
     3	import { useAuth } from '@/contexts/AuthContext';
     4	import { Card, CardContent, CardHeader, CardTitle } from '@/components/ui/card';
     5	import { Select, SelectContent, SelectItem, SelectTrigger, SelectValue } from '@/components/ui/select';
     6	import { Badge } from '@/components/ui/badge';
     7	import { Skeleton } from '@/components/ui/skeleton';
     8	import { Progress } from '@/components/ui/progress';
     9	import { toast } from 'sonner';
    10	import { BarChart2, TrendingUp, Star } from 'lucide-react';
    11	import type { AnonymousReview } from '@/types/types';
    12	import { DIMENSION_LABELS, DIMENSIONS, type ReviewDimensionKey } from '@/types/types';
    13	import { useMonthCycles } from '@/hooks/use-month-cycles';
    14	
    15	export default function StatsPage() {
    16	  const { profile } = useAuth();
    17	  const { cycles, loading: loadingCycles, currentCycle } = useMonthCycles(3);
    18	  const [selectedCycle, setSelectedCycle] = useState<string>('');
    19	  const [reviews, setReviews] = useState<AnonymousReview[]>([]);
    20	  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);
    21	
    22	  // cycles 加载完后默认选当前月
    23	  useEffect(() => {
    24	    if (!loadingCycles && currentCycle && !selectedCycle) {
    25	      setSelectedCycle(currentCycle.id);
    26	    }
    27	  }, [loadingCycles, currentCycle, selectedCycle]);
    28	
    29	  const fetchReviews = useCallback(async () => {
    30	    if (!selectedCycle || !profile) return;
    31	    setLoading(true);
    32	    const { data, error } = await supabase
    33	      .from('anonymous_reviews')
    34	      .select('*')
    35	      .eq('cycle_id', selectedCycle)
    36	      .eq('reviewee_id', profile.id);
    37	    if (error) {
    38	      toast.error('获取统计数据失败');
    39	    } else {
    40	      setReviews(Array.isArray(data) ? data : []);
    41	    }
    42	    setLoading(false);
    43	  }, [selectedCycle, profile]);
    44	
    45	  useEffect(() => {
    46	    fetchReviews();
    47	  }, [fetchReviews]);
    48	
    49	  // 计算各维度统计
    50	  const calcStats = (dim: ReviewDimensionKey) => {
    51	    const scores = reviews
    52	      .map((r) => r[`${dim}_score` as keyof AnonymousReview] as number | null)
    53	      .filter((s): s is number => s !== null && s > 0);
    54	    if (scores.length === 0) return { avg: null, count: 0, distribution: [0, 0, 0, 0, 0] };
    55	    const avg = scores.reduce((a, b) => a + b, 0) / scores.length;
    56	    const distribution = [1, 2, 3, 4, 5].map((star) => scores.filter((s) => s === star).length);
    57	    return { avg, count: scores.length, distribution };
    58	  };
    59	
    60	  const overallAvg = () => {
    61	    const allAvgs = DIMENSIONS.map((d) => calcStats(d).avg).filter((v): v is number => v !== null);
    62	    if (allAvgs.length === 0) return null;
    63	    return allAvgs.reduce((a, b) => a + b, 0) / allAvgs.length;
    64	  };
    65	
    66	  const overall = overallAvg();
    67	  const reviewCount = reviews.length;
    68	
    69	  const scoreColor = (score: number | null) => {
    70	    if (score === null) return 'text-muted-foreground';
    71	    if (score >= 4) return 'text-green-600';
    72	    if (score >= 3) return 'text-primary';
    73	    return 'text-destructive';
    74	  };
    75	
    76	  const starLabel = ['差', '较差', '一般', '良好', '优秀'];
    77	
    78	  return (
    79	    <div className="max-w-3xl mx-auto space-y-6">
    80	      <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
    81	        <BarChart2 className="w-5 h-5 text-primary" />
    82	        <div>
    83	          <h1 className="text-xl font-semibold text-balance">评价统计</h1>
    84	          <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">查看您在各评价周期的综合评分统计</p>
    85	        </div>
    86	      </div>
    87	
    88	      {/* 月份选择 */}
    89	      <Card className="shadow-card">
    90	        <CardContent className="py-4 flex flex-col md:flex-row md:items-center gap-3">
    91	          <span className="text-sm font-medium shrink-0">查看月份：</span>
    92	          {loadingCycles ? (
    93	            <Skeleton className="h-9 w-48 bg-muted" />
    94	          ) : (
    95	            <Select value={selectedCycle} onValueChange={setSelectedCycle}>
    96	              <SelectTrigger className="w-full md:w-56">
    97	                <SelectValue placeholder="请选择月份" />
    98	              </SelectTrigger>
    99	              <SelectContent>
   100	                {cycles.length === 0 ? (
   101	                  <SelectItem value="none" disabled>暂无数据</SelectItem>
   102	                ) : (
   103	                  cycles.map((c) => (
   104	                    <SelectItem key={c.id} value={c.id}>
   105	                      <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
   106	                        {c.name}
   107	                        {c.is_active && (
   108	                          <Badge variant="default" className="text-[10px] py-0">本月</Badge>
   109	                        )}
   110	                      </div>
   111	                    </SelectItem>
   112	                  ))
   113	                )}
   114	              </SelectContent>
   115	            </Select>
   116	          )}
   117	        </CardContent>
   118	      </Card>
   119	
   120	      {loading ? (
   121	        <div className="space-y-4">
   122	          {Array.from({ length: 3 }).map((_, i) => (
   123	            <Skeleton key={i} className="h-32 w-full bg-muted rounded-lg" />
   124	          ))}
   125	        </div>
   126	      ) : !selectedCycle ? (
   127	        <Card className="shadow-card">
   128	          <CardContent className="py-10 text-center text-muted-foreground text-sm">请选择评价周期</CardContent>
   129	        </Card>
   130	      ) : reviewCount === 0 ? (
   131	        <Card className="shadow-card">
   132	          <CardContent className="py-10 text-center">
   133	            <TrendingUp className="w-8 h-8 text-muted-foreground mx-auto mb-2" />
   134	            <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">该周期暂未收到任何评价</p>
   135	          </CardContent>
   136	        </Card>
   137	      ) : (
   138	        <>
   139	          {/* 综合概览 */}
   140	          <div className="grid grid-cols-2 md:grid-cols-3 gap-4">
   141	            <Card className="shadow-card h-full">
   142	              <CardContent className="py-4 text-center">
   143	                <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground mb-1">综合评分</p>
   144	                <p className={`text-3xl font-bold ${scoreColor(overall)}`}>
   145	                  {overall !== null ? overall.toFixed(1) : '—'}
   146	                </p>
   147	                <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground mt-1">满分 5.0</p>
   148	              </CardContent>
   149	            </Card>
   150	            <Card className="shadow-card h-full">
   151	              <CardContent className="py-4 text-center">
   152	                <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground mb-1">收到评价</p>
   153	                <p className="text-3xl font-bold text-primary">{reviewCount}</p>
   154	                <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground mt-1">条评价</p>
   155	              </CardContent>
   156	            </Card>
   157	            <Card className="shadow-card h-full col-span-2 md:col-span-1">
   158	              <CardContent className="py-4 text-center">
   159	                <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground mb-1">评分范围</p>
   160	                <div className="flex items-center justify-center gap-1">
   161	                  {[1, 2, 3, 4, 5].map((s) => (
   162	                    <Star
   163	                      key={s}
   164	                      className={`w-5 h-5 ${overall !== null && s <= Math.round(overall) ? 'text-yellow-400 fill-yellow-400' : 'text-muted-foreground'}`}
   165	                    />
   166	                  ))}
   167	                </div>
   168	                <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground mt-1">
   169	                  {overall !== null ? starLabel[Math.round(overall) - 1] : '暂无'}
   170	                </p>
   171	              </CardContent>
   172	            </Card>
   173	          </div>
   174	
   175	          {/* 各维度统计 */}
   176	          <div className="space-y-4">
   177	            {DIMENSIONS.map((dim) => {
   178	              const { avg, count, distribution } = calcStats(dim);
   179	              const maxCount = Math.max(...distribution, 1);
   180	              return (

   194	                    {/* 平均分进度条 */}

    41	        supabase
    42	          .from('profiles')
    43	          .select('id, username, display_name, role, created_at')
    44	          .order('display_name'),
    45	        supabase

    47	          .select('*')

    49	      ]);

    64	          const scores = userReviews
    65	            .map((r) => r[`${dim}_score` as keyof Review] as number | null)
    66	            .filter((s): s is number => s !== null && s > 0);
    67	          avgScores[dim] = scores.length > 0 ? scores.reduce((a, b) => a + b, 0) / scores.length : null;
    68	        }
    69	        return { profile, reviews: userReviews, avgScores };
    70	      });
    71	
    72	      setStats(revieweeStats);
    73	    } catch {
    74	      toast.error('加载数据失败');
    75	    }
    76	    setLoading(false);
    77	  }, [selectedCycle]);
    78	
    79	  useEffect(() => {
    80	    fetchStats();
    81	  }, [fetchStats]);

    85	    if (score >= 4) return 'text-green-600';
    86	    if (score >= 3) return 'text-primary';
    87	    return 'text-destructive';

   208	                            <span className="text-xs text-muted-foreground w-24 shrink-0">{DIMENSION_LABELS[dim]}</span>
   209	                            <Progress
   210	                              value={avg !== null ? (avg / 5) * 100 : 0}
   211	                              className="flex-1 h-1.5"
   212	                            />
   213	                            <span className={`text-xs font-semibold w-8 text-right shrink-0 ${scoreColor(avg)}`}>
   214	                              {avg !== null ? avg.toFixed(1) : '—'}
   215	                            </span>
   216	                          </div>
   217	                        );
   218	                      })}
   219	                    </div>
   220	                  </div>
   221	
   222	                  {/* 评价明细（含评价人，管理员可见） */}
   223	                  {item.reviews.length === 0 ? (
   224	                    <div className="px-4 py-4 text-center text-muted-foreground text-sm">该周期暂无评价</div>
   225	                  ) : (
   226	                    <div className="px-4 py-4 space-y-4">
   227	                      <p className="text-xs font-medium text-muted-foreground">评价明细（{item.reviews.length} 条，含评价人 · 仅管理员可见）</p>
   228	                      {item.reviews.map((review, idx) => (
   229	                        <ReviewDetailCard key={review.id} review={review} index={idx + 1} profiles={stats.map(s => s.profile)} />
   230	                      ))}
   231	                    </div>
   232	                  )}
   233	                </div>
   234	              )}
   235	            </Card>
   236	          ))}
   237	        </div>
   238	      )}
   239	    </div>
   240	  );
   241	}
   242	
   243	// 单条评价详情卡（展示评价人+各维度）
   244	function ReviewDetailCard({ review, index, profiles }: { review: Review; index: number; profiles: Profile[] }) {
   245	  const reviewer = profiles.find((p) => p.id === review.reviewer_id);
   246	  return (
   247	    <div className="rounded border border-border bg-card p-3">
   248	      <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mb-2">
   249	        <User className="w-3.5 h-3.5 text-muted-foreground" />
   250	        <span className="text-xs font-medium">
   251	          评价人：{reviewer ? (reviewer.display_name || reviewer.username) : '已删除用户'}
   252	        </span>
   253	        <span className="text-xs text-muted-foreground ml-auto">#{index}</span>
   254	      </div>
   255	      <Separator className="mb-2" />
   256	      <div className="space-y-1.5">

   259	          const note = review[`${dim}_note` as keyof Review] as string;
   260	          return (
   261	            <div key={dim} className="flex items-start gap-2 text-xs">
   262	              <span className="text-muted-foreground w-24 shrink-0">{DIMENSION_LABELS[dim]}</span>
   263	              <span className="font-medium text-primary">{score ? `${score}分` : '未评'}</span>
   264	              {note && <span className="text-muted-foreground flex-1 min-w-0 break-words">{note}</span>}
   265	            </div>
   266	          );
   267	        })}
   268	      </div>
   269	    </div>
   270	  );
   271	}

    12	export default function LoginPage() {
    13	  const [username, setUsername] = useState('');
    14	  const [password, setPassword] = useState('');

    16	  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);

    18	  const navigate = useNavigate();
    19	
    20	  const handleLogin = async (e: React.FormEvent) => {
    21	    e.preventDefault();
    22	    if (!username.trim() || !password.trim()) {
    23	      toast.error('请输入用户名和密码');
    24	      return;
    25	    }

    31	    const { error } = await signInWithUsername(username.trim(), password);
    32	    setLoading(false);

    35	    } else {
    36	      toast.success('登录成功');
    37	      // 跳转到根路由，由 DefaultRedirect 按角色分发落地页

     1	import React from 'react';
     2	import { BrowserRouter as Router, Routes, Route, Navigate } from 'react-router-dom';
     3	import IntersectObserver from '@/components/common/IntersectObserver';
     4	import { Toaster } from '@/components/ui/sonner';
     5	import { AuthProvider, useAuth } from '@/contexts/AuthContext';
     6	import { RouteGuard } from '@/components/common/RouteGuard';
     7	
     8	import LoginPage from '@/pages/LoginPage';
     9	import AppLayout from '@/components/layouts/AppLayout';
    10	import ReviewPage from '@/pages/ReviewPage';
    11	import MyReviewsPage from '@/pages/MyReviewsPage';
    12	import StatsPage from '@/pages/StatsPage';
    13	import UserManagementPage from '@/pages/admin/UserManagementPage';
    14	import CycleManagementPage from '@/pages/admin/CycleManagementPage';
    15	import GlobalStatsPage from '@/pages/admin/GlobalStatsPage';
    16	
    17	/** 根据角色决定默认落地页：可填写评价的角色优先进入填写页 */
    18	function DefaultRedirect() {
    19	  const { profile } = useAuth();
    20	  const role = profile?.role ?? 'reviewee_only';
    21	  const to = role === 'reviewer' || role === 'admin' ? '/review' : '/my-reviews';
    22	  return <Navigate to={to} replace />;
    23	}
    24	
    25	const App: React.FC = () => {
    26	  return (
    27	    <Router>
    28	      <AuthProvider>
    29	        <RouteGuard>
    30	          <IntersectObserver />
    31	          <Routes>
    32	            {/* 公开路由 */}
    33	            <Route path="/login" element={<LoginPage />} />
    34	
    35	            {/* 受保护的路由（嵌套在布局内）*/}
    36	            <Route path="/" element={<AppLayout />}>
    37	              <Route index element={<DefaultRedirect />} />
    38	              <Route path="review" element={<ReviewPage />} />
    39	              <Route path="my-reviews" element={<MyReviewsPage />} />
    40	              <Route path="stats" element={<StatsPage />} />
    41	              <Route path="admin/users" element={<UserManagementPage />} />
    42	              <Route path="admin/cycles" element={<CycleManagementPage />} />
    44	            </Route>
    45	
    46	            {/* 未匹配路由 */}
    47	            <Route path="*" element={<Navigate to="/" replace />} />
    48	          </Routes>
    49	          <Toaster />
    50	        </RouteGuard>
    51	      </AuthProvider>
    52	    </Router>
    53	  );
    54	};
    55	
    56	export default App;

     1	import { useEffect } from 'react';
     2	import { useNavigate, useLocation } from 'react-router-dom';
     3	import { useAuth } from '@/contexts/AuthContext';
     4	
     5	interface RouteGuardProps {
     6	  children: React.ReactNode;
     7	}
     8	
     9	const PUBLIC_ROUTES = ['/login'];
    10	
    11	export function RouteGuard({ children }: RouteGuardProps) {
    12	  const { user, loading } = useAuth();
    13	  const navigate = useNavigate();
    14	  const location = useLocation();
    15	
    16	  useEffect(() => {
    17	    if (loading) return;
    18	    const isPublic = PUBLIC_ROUTES.includes(location.pathname);
    19	    if (!user && !isPublic) {
    20	      navigate('/login', { state: { from: location.pathname }, replace: true });
    21	    }
    22	    // 已登录用户访问登录页，跳转到根路由由 DefaultRedirect 按角色分发
    23	    if (user && location.pathname === '/login') {
    24	      navigate('/', { replace: true });
    25	    }
    26	  }, [user, loading, location.pathname, navigate]);
    27	
    28	  if (loading) {
    29	    return (
    30	      <div className="flex items-center justify-center min-h-screen bg-background">
    31	        <div className="flex flex-col items-center gap-3">
    32	          <div className="w-10 h-10 border-2 border-primary border-t-transparent rounded-full animate-spin" />
    33	          <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">加载中...</p>
    34	        </div>
    35	      </div>
    36	    );
    37	  }
    38	
    39	  return <>{children}</>;
    40	}

```
import { createContext, useContext, useEffect, useState, type ReactNode } from 'react';
// @ts-ignore
import { supabase } from '@/db/supabase';
import type { User } from '@supabase/supabase-js';
// @ts-ignore
import type { Profile } from '@/types/types';
import { toast } from 'sonner';

export async function getProfile(userId: string): Promise<Profile | null> {
  const { data, error } = await supabase
    .from('profiles')
    .select('*')
    .eq('id', userId)
    .maybeSingle();

  if (error) {
    console.error('获取用户信息失败:', error);
    return null;
  }
  return data;
}
interface AuthContextType {
  user: User | null;
  profile: Profile | null;
  loading: boolean;
  signInWithUsername: (username: string, password: string) => Promise<{ error: Error | null }>;
  signUpWithUsername: (username: string, password: string) => Promise<{ error: Error | null }>;
  signOut: () => Promise<void>;
  refreshProfile: () => Promise<void>;
}

const AuthContext = createContext<AuthContextType | undefined>(undefined);

export function AuthProvider({ children }: { children: ReactNode }) {
  const [user, setUser] = useState<User | null>(null);
  const [profile, setProfile] = useState<Profile | null>(null);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);

  const refreshProfile = async () => {
    if (!user) {
      setProfile(null);
      return;
    }

    const profileData = await getProfile(user.id);
    setProfile(profileData);
  };

  useEffect(() => {
    supabase
      .auth
      .getSession()
      // @ts-ignore
      .then(({ data: { session } }) => {
        setUser(session?.user ?? null);
        if (session?.user) {
          getProfile(session.user.id).then(setProfile);
        }
      })
      // @ts-ignore
      .catch(error => {
        toast.error(`获取用户信息失败: ${error.message}`);
      })
      .finally(() => {
        setLoading(false);
      });

    // @ts-ignore
    // In this function, do NOT use any await calls. Use `.then()` instead to avoid deadlocks.
    const { data: { subscription } } = supabase.auth.onAuthStateChange((_event, session) => {
      setUser(session?.user ?? null);
      if (session?.user) {
        getProfile(session.user.id).then(setProfile);
      } else {
        setProfile(null);
      }
    });

    return () => subscription.unsubscribe();
  }, []);

  const signInWithUsername = async (username: string, password: string) => {
    try {
      const email = `${username}@miaoda.com`;
      const { error } = await supabase.auth.signInWithPassword({
        email,
        password,
      });

      if (error) throw error;
      return { error: null };
    } catch (error) {
      return { error: error as Error };
    }
  };

  const signUpWithUsername = async (username: string, password: string) => {
    try {
      const email = `${username}@miaoda.com`;
      const { error } = await supabase.auth.signUp({
        email,
        password,
      });

      if (error) throw error;
      return { error: null };
    } catch (error) {
      return { error: error as Error };
    }
  };

  const signOut = async () => {
    await supabase.auth.signOut();
    setUser(null);
    setProfile(null);
  };

  return (
    <AuthContext.Provider value={{ user, profile, loading, signInWithUsername, signUpWithUsername, signOut, refreshProfile }}>
      {children}
    </AuthContext.Provider>
  );
}

export function useAuth() {
  const context = useContext(AuthContext);
  if (context === undefined) {
    throw new Error('useAuth must be used within an AuthProvider');
  }
  return context;
}
```

New String: ```
import { createContext, useContext, useEffect, useState, type ReactNode } from 'react';
import { pb } from '@/db/pb';
import type { Profile } from '@/types/types';

// PocketBase 用户简化类型（替代 Supabase User）
export interface PBUser {
  id: string;
  email: string;
}

/** 从 profiles 集合获取用户档案（通过 user_id 关联字段） */
export async function getProfile(userId: string): Promise<Profile | null> {
  try {
    const record = await pb.collection('profiles').getFirstListItem<Record<string, string>>(
      `user_id="${userId}"`
    );
    return {
      id: record.id,
      username: record.username ?? '',
      display_name: record.display_name ?? record.username ?? '',
      role: (record.role as Profile['role']) ?? 'reviewee_only',
      created_at: record.created ?? record.created_at ?? '',
    };
  } catch {
    return null;
  }
}

interface AuthContextType {
  user: PBUser | null;
  profile: Profile | null;
  loading: boolean;
  /** identity 可以是完整邮箱（如 yi.zhou@smartmore.com）或用户名 */
  signInWithUsername: (identity: string, password: string) => Promise<{ error: Error | null }>;
  signUpWithUsername: (username: string, password: string) => Promise<{ error: Error | null }>;
  signOut: () => Promise<void>;
  refreshProfile: () => Promise<void>;
}

const AuthContext = createContext<AuthContextType | undefined>(undefined);

export function AuthProvider({ children }: { children: ReactNode }) {
  const [user, setUser] = useState<PBUser | null>(null);
  const [profile, setProfile] = useState<Profile | null>(null);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);

  const refreshProfile = async () => {
    const currentUser = pb.authStore.isValid ? (pb.authStore.model as { id: string } | null) : null;
    if (!currentUser) {
      setProfile(null);
      return;
    }
    const data = await getProfile(currentUser.id);
    setProfile(data);
  };

  // 初始化：从 PocketBase authStore 恢复登录态（token 自动持久化于 localStorage）
  useEffect(() => {
    const initAuth = async () => {
      if (pb.authStore.isValid && pb.authStore.model) {
        const model = pb.authStore.model as { id: string; email: string };
        setUser({ id: model.id, email: model.email ?? '' });
        const data = await getProfile(model.id);
        setProfile(data);
      }
      setLoading(false);
    };

    initAuth();

    // 监听 authStore 变化（登录/登出/token 过期）
    const unsubscribe = pb.authStore.onChange((token) => {
      if (token && pb.authStore.model) {
        const model = pb.authStore.model as { id: string; email: string };
        setUser({ id: model.id, email: model.email ?? '' });
        getProfile(model.id).then(setProfile);
      } else {
        setUser(null);
        setProfile(null);
      }
    });

    return () => unsubscribe();
  }, []);

  /**
   * 登录：直接使用完整邮箱或 PocketBase username，不拼接后缀。
   * 示例：yi.zhou@smartmore.com / 123123123
   */
  const signInWithUsername = async (identity: string, password: string) => {
    try {
      const authData = await pb.collection('users').authWithPassword(identity, password);
      const model = authData.record as { id: string; email: string };
      setUser({ id: model.id, email: model.email ?? '' });
      const data = await getProfile(model.id);
      setProfile(data);
      return { error: null };
    } catch (err) {
      console.error('PocketBase 登录失败:', err);
      return { error: err as Error };
    }
  };

  const signUpWithUsername = async (username: string, password: string) => {
    try {
      await pb.collection('users').create({
        username,
        password,
        passwordConfirm: password,
      });
      return { error: null };
    } catch (err) {
      return { error: err as Error };
    }
  };

  const signOut = async () => {
    pb.authStore.clear();
    setUser(null);
    setProfile(null);
  };

  return (
    <AuthContext.Provider value={{ user, profile, loading, signInWithUsername, signUpWithUsername, signOut, refreshProfile }}>
      {children}
    </AuthContext.Provider>
  );
}

export function useAuth() {
  const context = useContext(AuthContext);
  if (context === undefined) {
    throw new Error('useAuth must be used within an AuthProvider');
  }
  return context;
}
```

```
import { useState, useEffect, useCallback } from 'react';
```
```
import { pb } from '@/db/pb';
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { Input } from '@/components/ui/input';
import { Label } from '@/components/ui/label';
import { Badge } from '@/components/ui/badge';
import { Card, CardContent, CardHeader, CardTitle } from '@/components/ui/card';
import { Dialog, DialogContent, DialogHeader, DialogTitle, DialogFooter } from '@/components/ui/dialog';
import { AlertDialog, AlertDialogAction, AlertDialogCancel, AlertDialogContent, AlertDialogDescription, AlertDialogFooter, AlertDialogHeader, AlertDialogTitle } from '@/components/ui/alert-dialog';
```
