```
import { Skeleton } from '@/components/ui/skeleton';
import { toast } from 'sonner';
import { Plus, Pencil, Trash2, Users } from 'lucide-react';
import type { Profile, UserRole } from '@/types/types';
import { ROLE_LABELS, ROLE_DESCRIPTIONS } from '@/types/types';

/** 将 PocketBase records 映射为 Profile 类型 */
function toProfile(r: Record<string, string>): Profile {
  return {
    id: r.id,
    username: r.username ?? '',
    display_name: r.display_name ?? r.username ?? '',
    role: (r.role as UserRole) ?? 'reviewee_only',
    created_at: r.created ?? r.created_at ?? '',
  };
}

export default function UserManagementPage() {
  const [users, setUsers] = useState<Profile[]>([]);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
  const [createOpen, setCreateOpen] = useState(false);
  const [editTarget, setEditTarget] = useState<Profile | null>(null);
  const [deleteTarget, setDeleteTarget] = useState<Profile | null>(null);
  const [submitting, setSubmitting] = useState(false);

  // 表单状态
  const [form, setForm] = useState({
    username: '',
    display_name: '',
    password: '',
    role: 'reviewee_only' as UserRole,
  });

  const fetchUsers = useCallback(async () => {
    setLoading(true);
    try {
      const result = await pb.collection('profiles').getList<Record<string, string>>(1, 200, {
        sort: 'created',
      });
      setUsers(result.items.map(toProfile));
    } catch {
      toast.error('获取用户列表失败');
    }
    setLoading(false);
  }, []);

  useEffect(() => {
    fetchUsers();
  }, [fetchUsers]);

  const handleCreate = async () => {
    if (!form.username.trim() || !form.password.trim()) {
      toast.error('用户名和密码不能为空');
      return;
    }
    if (form.password.length < 6) {
      toast.error('密码长度至少6位');
      return;
    }
    setSubmitting(true);
    try {
      // 1. 在 PocketBase users 集合创建认证账户
      const authRecord = await pb.collection('users').create<Record<string, string>>({
        email: `${form.username.trim()}@smartmore.com`,
        username: form.username.trim(),
        password: form.password,
        passwordConfirm: form.password,
        emailVisibility: false,
      });
      // 2. 在 profiles 集合创建用户档案
      await pb.collection('profiles').create({
        user_id: authRecord.id,
        username: form.username.trim(),
        display_name: form.display_name.trim() || form.username.trim(),
        role: form.role,
      });
      toast.success('用户创建成功');
      setCreateOpen(false);
      setForm({ username: '', display_name: '', password: '', role: 'reviewee_only' });
      fetchUsers();
    } catch (err) {
      const msg = err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err);
      toast.error(`创建失败：${msg}`);
    }
    setSubmitting(false);
  };

  const handleEdit = async () => {
    if (!editTarget) return;
    setSubmitting(true);
    try {
      await pb.collection('profiles').update(editTarget.id, {
        display_name: form.display_name.trim() || editTarget.username,
        role: form.role,
      });
      toast.success('用户信息已更新');
      setEditTarget(null);
      fetchUsers();
    } catch (err) {
      const msg = err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err);
      toast.error(`更新失败：${msg}`);
    }
    setSubmitting(false);
  };

  const handleDelete = async () => {
    if (!deleteTarget) return;
    setSubmitting(true);
    try {
      await pb.collection('profiles').delete(deleteTarget.id);
      toast.success('用户已删除');
      setDeleteTarget(null);
      fetchUsers();
    } catch (err) {
      const msg = err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err);
      toast.error(`删除失败：${msg}`);
    }
    setSubmitting(false);
  };

  const openEdit = (user: Profile) => {
    setEditTarget(user);
    setForm({ username: user.username, display_name: user.display_name, password: '', role: user.role });
  };

  const roleVariant = (role: UserRole) => {
    if (role === 'admin') return 'default';
    if (role === 'reviewer') return 'secondary';
    return 'outline';
  };

  return (
    <div className="max-w-4xl mx-auto space-y-6">
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
        <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
          <Users className="w-5 h-5 text-primary" />
          <div>
            <h1 className="text-xl font-semibold text-balance">用户管理</h1>
            <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">管理系统用户及权限角色</p>
          </div>
        </div>
        <Button onClick={() => { setCreateOpen(true); setForm({ username: '', display_name: '', password: '', role: 'reviewee_only' }); }}>
          <Plus className="w-4 h-4 mr-2" />
          新增用户
        </Button>
      </div>

      <Card className="shadow-card">
        <CardHeader className="pb-3">
          <CardTitle className="text-base">用户列表（共 {users.length} 人）</CardTitle>
        </CardHeader>
        <CardContent className="p-0">
          {loading ? (
            <div className="p-4 space-y-3">
              {Array.from({ length: 4 }).map((_, i) => <Skeleton key={i} className="h-12 w-full bg-muted" />)}
            </div>
          ) : users.length === 0 ? (
            <div className="p-8 text-center text-muted-foreground text-sm">暂无用户</div>
          ) : (
            <div className="overflow-x-auto">
              <table className="w-full">
                <thead>
                  <tr className="border-b border-border bg-muted/40">
                    <th className="text-left text-xs font-medium text-muted-foreground px-4 py-2.5 whitespace-nowrap">显示名称</th>
                    <th className="text-left text-xs font-medium text-muted-foreground px-4 py-2.5 whitespace-nowrap">用户名</th>
                    <th className="text-left text-xs font-medium text-muted-foreground px-4 py-2.5 whitespace-nowrap">角色权限</th>
                    <th className="text-left text-xs font-medium text-muted-foreground px-4 py-2.5 whitespace-nowrap">注册时间</th>
                    <th className="text-right text-xs font-medium text-muted-foreground px-4 py-2.5 whitespace-nowrap">操作</th>
                  </tr>
                </thead>
                <tbody>
                  {users.map((user) => (
                    <tr key={user.id} className="border-b border-border last:border-0 hover:bg-muted/20 transition-colors">
                      <td className="px-4 py-3 whitespace-nowrap">
                        <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                          <div className="w-7 h-7 rounded-full bg-primary/10 flex items-center justify-center text-xs font-bold text-primary shrink-0">
                            {(user.display_name || user.username)[0].toUpperCase()}
                          </div>
                          <span className="text-sm font-medium">{user.display_name || user.username}</span>
                        </div>
                      </td>
                      <td className="px-4 py-3 whitespace-nowrap text-sm text-muted-foreground">{user.username}</td>
                      <td className="px-4 py-3 whitespace-nowrap">
                        <Badge variant={roleVariant(user.role)} className="text-xs">{ROLE_LABELS[user.role]}</Badge>
                      </td>
                      <td className="px-4 py-3 whitespace-nowrap text-xs text-muted-foreground">
                        {new Date(user.created_at).toLocaleDateString('zh-CN')}
                      </td>
                      <td className="px-4 py-3 whitespace-nowrap text-right">
                        <div className="flex items-center justify-end gap-1">
                          <Button variant="ghost" size="icon" className="h-8 w-8" onClick={() => openEdit(user)}>
                            <Pencil className="w-3.5 h-3.5" />
                          </Button>
                          <Button
                            variant="ghost"
                            size="icon"
                            className="h-8 w-8 text-destructive hover:text-destructive hover:bg-destructive/10"
                            onClick={() => setDeleteTarget(user)}
                          >
                            <Trash2 className="w-3.5 h-3.5" />
                          </Button>
                        </div>
                      </td>
                    </tr>
                  ))}
                </tbody>
              </table>
            </div>
          )}
        </CardContent>
      </Card>

      {/* 创建用户弹窗 */}
      <Dialog open={createOpen} onOpenChange={setCreateOpen}>
        <DialogContent className="max-w-[calc(100%-2rem)] md:max-w-lg">
          <DialogHeader>
            <DialogTitle>新增用户</DialogTitle>
          </DialogHeader>
          <div className="space-y-4 py-2">
            <div className="space-y-1.5">
              <Label className="text-sm font-normal">用户名 <span className="text-destructive">*</span></Label>
              <Input
                placeholder="仅字母、数字和下划线"
                value={form.username}
                onChange={(e) => setForm((f) => ({ ...f, username: e.target.value }))}
              />
            </div>
            <div className="space-y-1.5">
              <Label className="text-sm font-normal">显示名称</Label>
              <Input
                placeholder="用于界面展示，如：张三"
                value={form.display_name}
                onChange={(e) => setForm((f) => ({ ...f, display_name: e.target.value }))}
              />
            </div>
            <div className="space-y-1.5">
              <Label className="text-sm font-normal">密码 <span className="text-destructive">*</span></Label>
              <Input
                type="password"
                placeholder="至少6位"
                value={form.password}
                onChange={(e) => setForm((f) => ({ ...f, password: e.target.value }))}
              />
            </div>
            <div className="space-y-1.5">
              <Label className="text-sm font-normal">角色权限 <span className="text-destructive">*</span></Label>
              <Select value={form.role} onValueChange={(v) => setForm((f) => ({ ...f, role: v as UserRole }))}>
                <SelectTrigger>
                  <SelectValue />
                </SelectTrigger>
                <SelectContent>
                  {(Object.entries(ROLE_LABELS) as [UserRole, string][]).map(([value, label]) => (
                    <SelectItem key={value} value={value}>
                      <div>
                        <div className="font-medium">{label}</div>
                        <div className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">{ROLE_DESCRIPTIONS[value]}</div>
                      </div>
                    </SelectItem>
                  ))}
                </SelectContent>
              </Select>
            </div>
          </div>
          <DialogFooter>
            <Button variant="outline" onClick={() => setCreateOpen(false)} disabled={submitting}>取消</Button>
            <Button onClick={handleCreate} disabled={submitting}>{submitting ? '创建中...' : '创建用户'}</Button>
          </DialogFooter>
        </DialogContent>
      </Dialog>

      {/* 编辑用户弹窗 */}
      <Dialog open={!!editTarget} onOpenChange={(v) => !v && setEditTarget(null)}>
        <DialogContent className="max-w-[calc(100%-2rem)] md:max-w-lg">
          <DialogHeader>
            <DialogTitle>编辑用户：{editTarget?.display_name || editTarget?.username}</DialogTitle>
          </DialogHeader>
          <div className="space-y-4 py-2">
            <div className="space-y-1.5">
              <Label className="text-sm font-normal">显示名称</Label>
              <Input
                value={form.display_name}
                onChange={(e) => setForm((f) => ({ ...f, display_name: e.target.value }))}
              />
            </div>
            <div className="space-y-1.5">
              <Label className="text-sm font-normal">角色权限</Label>
              <Select value={form.role} onValueChange={(v) => setForm((f) => ({ ...f, role: v as UserRole }))}>
                <SelectTrigger>
                  <SelectValue />
                </SelectTrigger>
                <SelectContent>
                  {(Object.entries(ROLE_LABELS) as [UserRole, string][]).map(([value, label]) => (
                    <SelectItem key={value} value={value}>
                      <div>
                        <div className="font-medium">{label}</div>
                        <div className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">{ROLE_DESCRIPTIONS[value]}</div>
                      </div>
                    </SelectItem>
                  ))}
                </SelectContent>
              </Select>
            </div>
          </div>
          <DialogFooter>
            <Button variant="outline" onClick={() => setEditTarget(null)} disabled={submitting}>取消</Button>
            <Button onClick={handleEdit} disabled={submitting}>{submitting ? '保存中...' : '保存更改'}</Button>
          </DialogFooter>
        </DialogContent>
      </Dialog>

      {/* 删除确认 */}
      <AlertDialog open={!!deleteTarget} onOpenChange={(v) => !v && setDeleteTarget(null)}>
        <AlertDialogContent className="max-w-[calc(100%-2rem)] md:max-w-lg">
          <AlertDialogHeader>
            <AlertDialogTitle>确认删除用户？</AlertDialogTitle>
            <AlertDialogDescription>
              即将删除用户「{deleteTarget?.display_name || deleteTarget?.username}」，该操作不可恢复。
              用户的历史评价数据将保留。
            </AlertDialogDescription>
          </AlertDialogHeader>
          <AlertDialogFooter>
            <AlertDialogCancel disabled={submitting}>取消</AlertDialogCancel>
            <AlertDialogAction
              onClick={handleDelete}
              disabled={submitting}
              className="bg-destructive text-destructive-foreground hover:bg-destructive/90"
            >
              {submitting ? '删除中...' : '确认删除'}
            </AlertDialogAction>
          </AlertDialogFooter>
        </AlertDialogContent>
      </AlertDialog>
    </div>
  );
}
```

/** 将 PocketBase records 映射为 Profile 类型 */
function toProfile(r: Record<string, string>): Profile {
  return {
    id: r.id,
    username: r.username ?? '',
    display_name: r.display_name ?? r.username ?? '',
    role: (r.role as UserRole) ?? 'reviewee_only',
    created_at: r.created ?? r.created_at ?? '',
  };
}

export default function UserManagementPage() {
  const [users, setUsers] = useState<Profile[]>([]);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
  const [createOpen, setCreateOpen] = useState(false);
  const [editTarget, setEditTarget] = useState<Profile | null>(null);
  const [deleteTarget, setDeleteTarget] = useState<Profile | null>(null);
  const [submitting, setSubmitting] = useState(false);

  const [form, setForm] = useState({
    username: '',
    display_name: '',
    password: '',
    role: 'reviewee_only' as UserRole,
  });

  const fetchUsers = useCallback(async () => {
    setLoading(true);
    try {
      const result = await pb.collection('profiles').getList<Record<string, string>>(1, 200, {
        sort: 'created',
      });
      setUsers(result.items.map(toProfile));
